# OMNI OS — Progress Report

**Data snapshot:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.10-pre.4 CLOSED — NVMe driver image consumes the new BLK syscalls (`IpcCreateChannel + BlkRegister + BlkLookup`), continuing TASK-005 (NVMe live driver bring-up) of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.10-pre.4) `crates/omni-driver-nvme-image/src/main.rs` extended with a new 3-syscall block landing between the existing `IrqAttach (72)` and the bring-up FSM that consumes the kernel-side BLK registry the previous slice wired (P6.7.10-pre.3): (i) `IpcCreateChannel (20)` allocates a fresh kernel-owned channel via the legacy MB12 fast-path (both signed tokens = 0; `BLK_CHANNEL_QUEUE_DEPTH = 1024`, `BackpressurePolicy::Block`, `tee_bound = false`) and stores the returned `ChannelId` (`u64::MAX → EXIT_IPC_CREATE_FAILED = 100`); (ii) `BlkRegister (76)` records the `omni.svc.blk.nvme0` → `channel_id` mapping by passing `NVME_DISK_SLOT = b"nvme0"` + the freshly-allocated channel id — the kernel verifies the caller owns `channel_id` (we just created it, so the ownership check passes by construction); (iii) `BlkLookup (78)` round-trips the registration as a defence-in-depth check (`ENOENT → EXIT_BLK_LOOKUP_NOT_FOUND = 131`; `channel_id` mismatch → `EXIT_BLK_LOOKUP_MISMATCH = 132`) so a kernel-registry regression aborts the driver before any FSM advance instead of silently mis-routing future filesystem requests. New syscall-number constants (`SYS_IPC_CREATE_CHANNEL = 20`, `SYS_BLK_REGISTER = 76`, `SYS_BLK_LOOKUP = 78`), BLK channel constants (`NVME_DISK_SLOT`, `BLK_CHANNEL_QUEUE_DEPTH`, `BLK_CHANNEL_BACKPRESSURE_BLOCK`, `BLK_CHANNEL_TEE_NOT_BOUND`), and 4 new sentinel exit codes (`EXIT_IPC_CREATE_FAILED = 100`, `EXIT_BLK_REGISTER_BASE = 110`, `EXIT_BLK_LOOKUP_NOT_FOUND = 131`, `EXIT_BLK_LOOKUP_MISMATCH = 132`). Module documentation extended with steps 7–9 + 10–11 covering the new `IpcCreateChannel`/`BlkRegister`/`BlkLookup`/`FSM`/`TaskExit` ordering. The byte-slice `NVME_DISK_SLOT: &[u8] = b"nvme0"` avoids the `PanicOnAlloc` global-allocator panic that a `String` would trigger inside this `no_std + no_main` ELF. Build Info panel (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/demo.rs::render_buildinfo`): Active=`P6.7.10-pre.4 NVMe BLK wire` (cyan), Next=`P6.7.10-pre.5 NVMe admin queue`, Phase=`1 - Microkernel POC  (~99.97%)`, Tests=`1277 workspace pass`. **Acceptance gates**: `cargo fmt --all -- --check` clean. `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets --all-features -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy -p omni-kernel --target x86_64-unknown-none --features bare-metal -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy -p omni-kernel --target x86_64-unknown-none --features bare-metal,mb12-userprobe -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy --manifest-path kernel-runner/Cargo.toml --target x86_64-unknown-none -- -D warnings` clean. Clippy 3 driver-image siblings (`x86_64-unknown-none --release`) clean. `bash scripts/check-no-blanket-allow.sh` → `ok (scanned 16 crate-root files)`. `RUSTDOCFLAGS=-Dwarnings cargo doc -p omni-kernel --features bare-metal --target x86_64-unknown-none --no-deps` clean. `RUSTDOCFLAGS=-Dwarnings cargo doc --workspace --no-deps --all-features` clean. `python3 scripts/lint-oips.py` → `0 error(s), 0 warning(s) across 19 file(s)`. Workspace test count stable at **1277 pass / 0 fail** — the new code is `no_main` ELF entry path that cannot be unit-tested in-crate; coverage relies on the kernel-side host tests landed in P6.7.10-pre.3 (`errno_for_*` × 7 + `kernel_syscall_dispatch_blk_numbers_translate_to_blk_variants` × 1) plus the Proxmox boot smoke. **No new dependency** — `omni-driver-shared` was already a workspace member and provides the cap-token lookups used by the existing `MmioMap`/`DmaMap`/`IrqAttach` triplet. **Stato P6.7**: P6.7.0/1/2/2.bis/3/3.bis/4/5/6/7/8.0/8.1/8.2/8.3/8.4/8.5/8.6/8.7/8.8/8.9/8.10/9-pre.0..9-pre.11 + 10-pre.1 + 10-pre.2 + 10-pre.3 + **10-pre.4** chiusi. **TASK-010 (VT-d / AMD-Vi IOMMU backends) CLOSED**. **TASK-005 (NVMe live driver bring-up) IN PROGRESS — pre.4 di N**. **P6.7.10-pre.5 (NVMe admin queue scaffold — `omni-driver-nvme::bringup` Admin SQ/CQ allocation + `CC.EN=1` per OIP-014 § S6 step 6, gated by `IpcSend` against the new BLK channel for trace events) prossimo**. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.10-pre.3 CLOSED — kernel-side BLK registry syscalls (`BlkRegister (76)` / `BlkUnregister (77)` / `BlkLookup (78)`) + task-exit clean-up wired, continuing TASK-005 (NVMe live driver bring-up) of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.10-pre.3) Three new syscalls land in the `7x` driver-framework decade per OIP-Driver-NVMe-014 § S4 + § S6 step 12, bridging the kernel-internal `BlkChannelRegistry` (landed P6.7.10-pre.2) to user space through the rich two-register return path (`SyscallReturn { rax, rdx }`): `BlkRegister (76)` accepts `(disk_slot_ptr, disk_slot_len, channel_id, 0, 0, 0)` and records the canonical `omni.svc.blk.<disk_slot>` mapping after verifying the caller owns the supplied `ChannelId` in the live `IpcRegistry` (mismatch → `EACCES`, unknown id → `EINVAL`); `BlkUnregister (77)` accepts `(disk_slot_ptr, disk_slot_len, 0, 0, 0, 0)` and delegates to `BlkChannelRegistry::unregister` which already enforces owner-only teardown (`OwnerMismatch → EACCES`); `BlkLookup (78)` accepts `(disk_slot_ptr, disk_slot_len, 0, 0, 0, 0)` and returns the live `channel_id` in `rax` on success or `(0, ENOENT)` on miss — read-only because the channel id alone confers no IPC authority (`IpcSend` / `IpcRecv` still require the per-channel capability tokens minted at create time). New `crates/omni-kernel/src/services/blk.rs` additions: process-global `static mut BLK_REGISTRY: BlkChannelRegistry = BlkChannelRegistry::new()` (gated on `bare-metal` + `target_arch = "x86_64"`, mirroring the `IPC_REGISTRY` singleton pattern — single-CPU + interrupt-masked SYSCALL provides the no-aliasing invariant per ADR-0005), `blk_registry_mut() -> &'static mut BlkChannelRegistry` + `blk_registry() -> &'static BlkChannelRegistry` accessors (both `unsafe fn`, `SAFETY` documented at the fn boundary), and a host-callable `errno_for(BlkRegistryError) -> u64` mapper that publishes the POSIX-aligned errno taxonomy (`DiskSlotEmpty | DiskSlotTooLong | DiskSlotInvalidChar → EINVAL`; `DiskSlotAlreadyRegistered → EEXIST`; `RegistryFull → ENOSPC`; `DiskSlotNotRegistered → ENOENT`; `OwnerMismatch → EACCES`; defensive `Internal → EIO`). `crates/omni-kernel/src/syscall.rs` extended with three new `SyscallNumber` discriminants (`BlkRegister = 76`, `BlkUnregister = 77`, `BlkLookup = 78`) and three new errno constants in `syscall_errno` (`ENOENT = 2`, `EIO = 5`, `EEXIST = 17`). `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs` extended with the dedicated `blk_handlers` module (gated on the bare-metal triple `feature = "bare-metal" + target_os = "none" + not(test)`): `copy_user_disk_slot` validates the user pointer (`EFAULT` on out-of-user-half / null with non-zero len) then bounds the length (`EINVAL` on empty / oversized) then decodes UTF-8 (the registry's allowed alphabet is ASCII so UTF-8 is a superset and the path is cheap); `check_channel_owner` verifies `ipc_registry().channel(channel_id).owner == caller_task`; three handlers (`blk_register` / `blk_unregister` / `blk_lookup`) chain validation → ownership check → registry mutation; `tear_down_blk_channels(task)` drains `BLK_REGISTRY` for the exiting owner, invoked from `task_exit` AFTER the existing `tear_down_mmio_mappings` / `tear_down_dma_mappings` / `tear_down_irq_attachments` / `tear_down_pci_bindings` chain so a crashed/killed driver does not leak stale registry entries on PCB retire. Dispatcher routing: new `BlkRegister | BlkUnregister | BlkLookup` arms added to the legacy `dispatch` `CapabilityDenied` group (rich-path-only convention — same as `MmioMap | DmaMap | IrqAttach | DriverLoad`), three new arms in `dispatch_full` route to the live handlers, and three new arms in `kernel_syscall_dispatch (extern "C")` translate the wire-level `u32` numbers `76 → SyscallNumber::BlkRegister`, `77 → ::BlkUnregister`, `78 → ::BlkLookup`. **+8 new host-side tests**: 7 in `omni_kernel::services::blk::tests::*` (`errno_for_argument_shape_violations_maps_to_einval`, `errno_for_duplicate_slot_maps_to_eexist`, `errno_for_capacity_ceiling_maps_to_enospc`, `errno_for_lookup_failed_maps_to_enoent`, `errno_for_owner_mismatch_maps_to_eacces`, `errno_for_internal_invariant_maps_to_eio`, `errno_for_is_total_over_known_variants` tripwire), 1 in `omni_kernel::bare_metal::syscall_entry::tests::*` (`kernel_syscall_dispatch_blk_numbers_translate_to_blk_variants` exercises the 76/77/78 → `SyscallNumber` arm explicitly). Existing host-side tests extended: `syscall_numbers_are_stable` pins the three new discriminants; `syscall_errno_codes_are_posix_aligned` pins the three new errno constants; `dispatcher_full_dma_map_irq_attach_and_driver_load_surface_eaccess_on_host` + `kernel_syscall_dispatch_driver_framework_numbers_route` + `dispatcher_driver_framework_legacy_arm_returns_capability_denied` extended to cover the BLK triplet; `kernel_syscall_dispatch_unknown_driver_decade_number_returns_sentinel` narrowed to `79` (the only number inside `7x` still reserved-but-unallocated). Workspace test count 1269 → **1277 pass / 0 fail** (`cargo test --workspace --all-features -- --test-threads=1`). **Build Info panel** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/demo.rs::render_buildinfo`): Active=`P6.7.10-pre.3 BLK syscalls` (cyan), Next=`P6.7.10-pre.4 NVMe driver image`, Phase=`1 - Microkernel POC  (~99.97%)`, Tests=`1277 workspace pass`. **Acceptance gates**: `cargo fmt --all -- --check` clean. `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets --all-features -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy -p omni-kernel --target x86_64-unknown-none --features bare-metal -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy -p omni-kernel --target x86_64-unknown-none --features bare-metal,mb12-userprobe -- -D warnings` clean. `cargo clippy --manifest-path kernel-runner/Cargo.toml --target x86_64-unknown-none -- -D warnings` clean. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.10-pre.2 CLOSED — kernel-side BLK channel registry landed in `omni-kernel`, continuing TASK-005 (NVMe live driver bring-up) of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.10-pre.2) Two new files under `crates/omni-kernel/src/services/`: `mod.rs` declares the `services` submodule tree, gated behind `#[cfg(feature = "bare-metal")]` so the surface is only compiled when the kernel framework that consumes it is in scope; `blk.rs` declares the canonical kernel-side BLK channel registry per OIP-Driver-NVMe-014 § S4 + § S6 step 12. The registry maps disk slot (`"nvme0"`, `"sata0"`, …) → live `ChannelId` so future filesystem services and capability-gated multiplexers can resolve `omni.svc.blk.<diskN>` without sniffing the kernel IPC layer by string — the IPC layer remains name-agnostic (channels addressed by `ChannelId` only). `BlkChannelRegistry` exposes `register(disk_slot, channel_id, owner) -> Result<&str, BlkRegistryError>` (returns the canonical channel name pre-built once at insertion so consumer call sites do not re-allocate on every lookup), `unregister(disk_slot, owner) -> Result<BlkChannelEntry, BlkRegistryError>` (owner-only teardown; `swap_remove` keeps average remove path O(1)), `lookup_disk_slot(&str)` / `lookup_channel_name(&str)` / `lookup_channel_id(ChannelId)` (all `Option<&BlkChannelEntry>`), `clear_for_owner(TaskId) -> usize` (task-exit drain — returns number of entries removed). Storage is `Vec<BlkChannelEntry>` (insertion-ordered until first `unregister`, capped at `MAX_BLK_CHANNELS = 64`). Per-slot allocation bounded by `MAX_DISK_SLOT_LEN = 32`. Disk-slot validator restricts the alphabet to `[A-Za-z0-9_-]` and rejects empty / oversized / non-ASCII / control-byte (newline, CR, escape) / dot inputs — closes a path where a compromised driver could embed log-line forgeries (CRLF, ANSI escapes) into the kernel boot log through the channel name. `BlkRegistryError::{DiskSlotEmpty, DiskSlotTooLong, DiskSlotInvalidChar, DiskSlotAlreadyRegistered, RegistryFull, DiskSlotNotRegistered, OwnerMismatch, Internal}` (`#[non_exhaustive]` — backward-compatible variant additions land via PR per the same OIP-014 § S7 policy already adopted by `BlkRequest` / `BlkResponse`). `Internal` exists only as a defensive sentinel for invariants the registry expects to hold but cannot statically prove (e.g. a `Vec` that should be non-empty immediately after `push`) — never returned in well-formed code; surfaces an error rather than panicking so the registry never aborts the kernel. Consumes `omni_types::blk::CHANNEL_NAME_PREFIX` so the prefix stays single-sourced across the two crates. `lib.rs` extended with `#[cfg(feature = "bare-metal")] pub mod services;`. **+32 new host-side tests** under `omni_kernel::services::blk::tests::*`: 5 construction & constant tripwires (`new_registry_is_empty`, `default_matches_new`, `max_disk_slot_len_constant_is_32`, `max_blk_channels_constant_is_64`, `channel_name_prefix_constant_matches_omni_types`); 12 `register` cases (`register_inserts_entry_with_canonical_channel_name`, `register_return_value_is_canonical_channel_name`, `register_accepts_alphanumeric_underscore_and_hyphen`, `register_rejects_empty_disk_slot`, `register_rejects_disk_slot_too_long`, `register_accepts_disk_slot_at_max_length`, `register_rejects_disk_slot_with_space`, `register_rejects_disk_slot_with_dot`, `register_rejects_disk_slot_with_control_byte`, `register_rejects_disk_slot_with_non_ascii`, `register_rejects_duplicate_disk_slot`, `register_rejects_when_registry_is_full`); 4 `unregister` cases (`unregister_drops_entry_and_returns_record`, `unregister_unknown_disk_slot_returns_not_registered`, `unregister_rejects_non_owner`, `re_register_after_unregister_succeeds`); 6 lookup cases (`lookup_disk_slot_returns_some_for_registered_slot`, `lookup_disk_slot_returns_none_for_unknown_slot`, `lookup_channel_name_uses_fully_qualified_name`, `lookup_channel_name_returns_none_for_missing_prefix`, `lookup_channel_id_finds_entry`, `lookup_channel_id_returns_none_for_unknown_id`); 3 `clear_for_owner` cases (`clear_for_owner_drops_all_owner_entries`, `clear_for_owner_with_no_match_returns_zero`, `clear_for_owner_on_empty_registry_is_noop`); 2 ordering cases (`entries_preserves_insertion_order_before_unregister`, `unregister_swap_remove_does_not_corrupt_remaining_entries`). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.10-pre.1 CLOSED — BLK service-channel ABI types landed in `omni-types`, opening TASK-005 (NVMe live bring-up) of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.10-pre.1) New `crates/omni-types/src/blk.rs` module declares the canonical wire shape of the generic block (BLK) service channel (`omni.svc.blk.<diskN>`) per OIP-Driver-NVMe-014 § M3 / § S4, the contract every storage driver MUST present so that file systems mediate against one shape (NVMe today, future SATA / virtio-blk / software RAID). Two `#[non_exhaustive]` `serde`-derived enums — `BlkRequest::{Read{lba,count,buf_iova}, Write{lba,count,buf_iova}, Flush, Discard{lba,count}}` and `BlkResponse::{Ok, NotSupported, DeviceError(u16), OutOfRange, InvalidArgument}` — mirror § M3 verbatim and lock the postcard discriminant order via tests (`*_variants_are_distinguishable_on_the_wire` asserts the first byte of each encoded variant). Per OIP-014 § S7 both enums opt into backward-compatible variant addition via `#[non_exhaustive]`. Four public `pub const`s anchor the contract for downstream consumers: `NON_NVME_DEVICE_ERROR = 0xFFFF` (non-NVMe sentinel; cannot collide with any real NVMe status word per NVMe 1.4 § 4.5), `MAX_BLOCK_COUNT_PER_REQUEST = 2048` (PRP-page ceiling per OIP-014 § S2), `BLOCK_SIZE_BYTES = 4096` (`LBADS = 12` per OIP-014 § M4 + § S6 step 10), `CHANNEL_NAME_PREFIX = "omni.svc.blk."` (capability-gate prefix the future kernel BLK registry will consume). All encoding routes through `omni_types::wire::encode_canonical` / `decode_canonical` — the single workspace audit point per OIP-Serde-004; no direct `postcard::*` calls anywhere. **+24 new host-side tests** under `omni_types::blk::tests::*`: 4 `BlkRequest` round-trips (`blk_request_read_round_trip`, `blk_request_write_round_trip`, `blk_request_flush_round_trip`, `blk_request_discard_round_trip`); 6 `BlkResponse` round-trips (`blk_response_ok_round_trip`, `blk_response_not_supported_round_trip`, `blk_response_device_error_nvme_status_round_trip`, `blk_response_device_error_non_nvme_sentinel_round_trip` — verifies `0xFFFF` survives, `blk_response_out_of_range_round_trip`, `blk_response_invalid_argument_round_trip`); 4 wire invariants (`blk_request_encoding_is_deterministic`, `blk_response_encoding_is_deterministic`, `blk_request_decode_rejects_trailing_bytes`, `blk_request_decode_rejects_truncated_input`, `blk_response_decode_rejects_empty_input`); 4 constants tripwires (`non_nvme_device_error_constant_is_0xffff`, `max_block_count_per_request_matches_prp_capacity`, `block_size_bytes_matches_oip_014_lbads_12`, `channel_name_prefix_matches_oip_014_s4`); 4 discriminator + encoding-shape checks (`blk_request_variants_are_distinguishable_on_the_wire`, `blk_response_variants_are_distinguishable_on_the_wire`, `blk_request_flush_encodes_to_single_byte`, `blk_response_ok_encodes_to_single_byte`); 2 cross-variant integration (`round_trip_request_then_response_share_no_state`, plus the wire-invariant suite). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.9-pre.11 CLOSED — live IOMMU per-device DTE / Context-Entry install + `GCMD.TE` / `CTRL.IommuEn` flip, closing TASK-010 of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.9-pre.11) **VT-d per-bus context-table refcounted allocator** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/vtd.rs`): new `BusContextTable { bus: u8, phys: u64, refcount: u32 }` struct + `VtdBackend::bus_context_tables: Vec<BusContextTable>` field. New methods `acquire_bus_context_table(bus, src) -> Result<u64, VtdAttachError>` (lazy 4-KiB-aligned alloc through `pt_alloc::FrameSource`; misaligned-frame defence returns the page to `src` and surfaces `BusContextAllocFailed`) and `release_bus_context_table(bus, src) -> Result<(), BusContextTableReleaseError>` (decrement refcount; `swap_remove` + `free_frame` when refcount==0). Accessors `bus_context_tables() -> &[BusContextTable]`, `bus_context_table_phys(bus) -> Option<u64>`, `bus_context_table_refcount(bus) -> Option<u32>`. New error variant `VtdAttachError::BusContextAllocFailed → IommuError::DomainTableFull`. **VT-d translation-enable** (vtd.rs): new `translation_enabled: bool` field + `is_translation_enabled() -> bool` accessor + `enable_translation(phys_offset) -> Result<(), VtdActivateError>` `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` method that writes `GCMD.TE` and polls `GSTS.TES` with bounded retry; new `VtdActivateError::TranslationEnableTimeout` variant; idempotent on re-call. **VT-d managed install + release** (vtd.rs): new `install_device_entry_with_alloc(phys_off, bdf, domain, slpt_phys, width, translation, src) -> Result<u64, VtdAttachError>` `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` wrapper that acquires the per-bus context table via `src`, then calls `install_device_entry` with that ctx-table phys; rolls back the refcount on `install_device_entry` failure so the bookkeeping stays consistent. Symmetric `release_device_entry_with_alloc(phys_off, bdf, src) -> Result<(), BusContextTableReleaseError>` zeroes the device's context entry, submits per-domain context-cache + IOTLB invalidate descriptors (best-effort drain), decrements bus refcount, and (when refcount==0) zeroes the root-table entry for the bus AND frees the ctx-table page via `release_bus_context_table`. **AMD-Vi translation-enable** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/amdvi.rs`): new `translation_enabled: bool` field + `is_translation_enabled() -> bool` accessor + `enable_translation(phys_offset) -> Result<(), AmdViActivateError>` `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` method that read-modify-writes `CTRL` to OR in `CTRL_BIT_IOMMU_EN` (preserving `CMD_BUF_EN | EVENT_LOG_EN` from activation), then submits `INVALIDATE_ALL` via `submit_cmd_descriptor` and waits for the command-buffer head to drain. New `AmdViActivateError::TranslationEnableTimeout` variant; idempotent on re-call. AMD-Vi needs no per-bus context tables (flat device table already allocated by `prepare_amd_vi_unit`). **Module-level dispatch** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/mod.rs`): new `iommu_translation_enabled() -> bool` host-callable accessor (dispatches via `with_iommu_backend`; returns `false` for passthrough). New `iommu_enable_translation(phys_offset) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` that returns `Ok(true)` on Intel/AMD success, `Ok(false)` on passthrough. New `install_vt_d_device_entry_managed(phys_off, bdf, domain, slpt_phys, width, translation, src) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` and `release_vt_d_device_entry_managed(phys_off, bdf, src) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` — both `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]`, wrapping the new VtdBackend methods through `with_iommu_backend`. **driver_load wiring** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs::driver_load_handlers::driver_load`): after the existing P6.7.9-pre.10 PT root provisioning, a new `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` block (gated on `any_bdf_attached && iommu_domain_pt_root_phys(domain).is_some()`) clones `pcb.bound_pci_devices`, builds a `KernelFrameSource`, and for each BDF dispatches on `iommu_vendor()`: Intel → `install_vt_d_device_entry_managed` (defaults: `AddressWidth::Bits48Level4`, `TranslationType::UntranslatedAndTranslated`), AMD → `install_amd_vi_device_entry` (defaults: `IommuFlags::READ|WRITE`, `PageMode::Level4`), Passthrough → `Ok(false)` no-op. After at least one `Ok(true)` install, calls `iommu_enable_translation(phys_off)` — idempotent across subsequent driver loads, flipping `GCMD.TE` / `CTRL.IommuEn` only the first time. Best-effort: failures are silently logged via the install return value but never propagate to user space — partial install state is observable because the IOMMU rejects DMA from un-DTE'd BDFs the moment TE/IommuEn is observed, so the driver's first `DmaMap` will EACCES out of the cap-check or IOMMU PF handler. **tear_down_pci_bindings symmetric release** (syscall_entry.rs): refactored to (a) drain `bound_pci_devices` upfront, (b) on `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` + `iommu_vendor() == Intel`, walk the BDF list and call `release_vt_d_device_entry_managed` for each (returns the per-bus ctx-table page when refcount==0), (c) drop the trait-level attachment via `iommu_detach_device` for every drained BDF, (d) release the per-domain PT root via `iommu_release_domain_pt` if provisioned. AMD-Vi falls back to the existing detach (no per-bus refcount to maintain). **+21 new host-side tests**: 12 in `bare_metal::iommu::vtd::tests::*` (`vtd_attach_error_bus_context_alloc_failed_maps_to_domain_table_full`, `fresh_backend_has_no_bus_context_tables`, `acquire_bus_context_table_allocates_on_first_call`, `acquire_bus_context_table_shares_page_across_repeat_acquires`, `acquire_bus_context_table_allocates_distinct_pages_per_bus`, `acquire_bus_context_table_surfaces_frame_alloc_failure`, `acquire_bus_context_table_rejects_misaligned_frame_and_returns_it`, `release_bus_context_table_decrements_refcount_then_frees`, `release_bus_context_table_unknown_bus_returns_err`, `release_bus_context_table_isolates_other_buses`, `reacquire_after_release_allocates_fresh_page`, `fresh_backend_is_not_translation_enabled` + `vtd_activate_error_translation_enable_timeout_maps_to_activation_failed` + `prepare_activation_with_different_params_resets_translation_enabled`); 3 in `bare_metal::iommu::amdvi::tests::*` (`fresh_backend_is_not_translation_enabled`, `amdvi_activate_error_translation_enable_timeout_maps_to_activation_failed`, `prepare_activation_with_different_params_resets_translation_enabled`); 4 in `bare_metal::iommu::tests::*` (`iommu_translation_enabled_false_for_passthrough`, `iommu_translation_enabled_false_for_fresh_intel_backend`, `iommu_translation_enabled_false_for_fresh_amd_backend`, `install_backend_for_vendor_resets_translation_enabled_flag`). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-22 (**P6.7.9-pre.10 CLOSED — IOMMU per-domain PT root provisioning wired into `DriverLoad` per TASK-010 of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (P6.7.9-pre.10) New `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/kernel_frame_source.rs` module: `KernelFrameSource<'a, const N: usize>` adapter wraps `&'a mut BitmapFrameAllocator<N>` + the bootloader direct-map offset and implements `pt_alloc::FrameSource`. On bare-metal `alloc_zeroed_frame()` (a) calls `BitmapFrameAllocator::alloc_frame`, (b) defensively validates 4-KiB alignment (returns the frame to the pool and surfaces `None` on mismatch — belt-and-braces vs. the allocator's invariant), (c) zero-fills the page via `core::ptr::write_bytes` through the direct map at `phys_offset.wrapping_add(phys)`, (d) returns the physical address. On host (`cfg(target_os != "none")`) the zero-fill step is elided because tests never dereference the returned address. `free_frame(phys)` routes through `BitmapFrameAllocator::free_frame` (alignment + bounds + double-free guards inherited). `bare_metal::iommu::mod` re-exports `KernelFrameSource` for ergonomic import. **`driver_load` handler extended** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs::driver_load_handlers::driver_load`): after the existing P6.7.9-pre.8 per-BDF attach loop, a new `any_bdf_attached` flag drives a single call to `iommu_provision_domain_pt(domain_for_task(task_id.0), &mut KernelFrameSource::new(fa, phys_off))` — best-effort (failures swallowed; the driver process stays alive but its first `DmaMap` will EACCES if the IOMMU is live and the root is missing). The block is `#[allow(unsafe_code)]`-gated for the `addr_of_mut!(FRAME_ALLOC)` reborrow with the standard single-CPU SAFETY rationale. **`tear_down_pci_bindings` extended**: after the per-BDF detach pass, `iommu_domain_pt_root_phys(domain)` is consulted; if `Some(_)` the helper builds a fresh `KernelFrameSource` and calls `iommu_release_domain_pt(domain, &mut src)` to return the 4-KiB root frame to `FRAME_ALLOC`. The `Some` gate keeps the `FRAME_ALLOC` reborrow scope tight on passthrough builds (and on processes that never provisioned). Phase-1 model: one IOMMU domain per driver process via `domain_for_task(task_id.0) -> DomainId`. **+6 new host-side tests** under `bare_metal::iommu::kernel_frame_source::tests::*` (`alloc_returns_aligned_frame_from_pool` — adapter alloc returns a 4-KiB-aligned frame and decrements the bitmap pool; `alloc_exhausts_pool_then_returns_none` — adapter surfaces `None` when the bitmap is empty; `free_returns_frame_to_pool_for_reuse` — first-fit re-uses the just-freed slot; `provision_through_domain_page_tables_round_trips` — end-to-end with `DomainPageTables::provision`/`release`; `provision_surfaces_pool_exhaustion_as_frame_alloc_failed` — empty allocator + provision maps to `DomainPtError::FrameAllocFailed`; `release_then_reprovision_distinct_domain_reuses_pool` — freed frame round-trips through a different domain). (P6.7.9-pre.9) New `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/pt_alloc.rs` module: vendor-neutral `FrameSource` trait (`alloc_zeroed_frame() -> Option<u64>` + `free_frame(phys: u64)`); `DomainPageTables` registry mapping `DomainId → root_phys` over a `Vec<DomainPtEntry>` with O(N) lookup, `provision(domain, &mut dyn FrameSource) -> Result<u64, DomainPtError>` (alloc-then-validate-alignment-defensively-then-record; misaligned frames are returned to the pool before surfacing `Misaligned`), `release(domain, &mut dyn FrameSource) -> Result<(), DomainPtError>`, `root_phys(domain) -> Option<u64>`, `is_provisioned(domain)`, `entries()`, `provisioned_count()`. `DomainPtError::{FrameAllocFailed, Misaligned, AlreadyProvisioned, NotProvisioned}` taxonomy. `MockFrameSource` (`cfg(test)`-only) hands out deterministic 4-KiB-aligned frames from `0x1_0000_0000`, tracks `(alloc, free)` call counters, recorded freed list, plus `force_alloc_fail` + `force_next_phys` override knobs to exercise the failure / misalignment paths. `VtdBackend` + `AmdViBackend` embed `domain_pts: DomainPageTables` and expose `provision_domain_pt` / `release_domain_pt` / `domain_pt_root_phys` / `domain_pt_entries` accessors symmetric across vendors. Module-level dispatch in `iommu/mod.rs`: `iommu_provision_domain_pt(domain, src)` / `iommu_release_domain_pt(domain, src)` / `iommu_domain_pt_root_phys(domain)` route through `IommuKind` — `Passthrough` short-circuits to `Ok(0)` / `Ok(())` / `None` without touching `src` so callers can drive the same code path on platforms without an IOMMU. **+19 new host-side tests**: 13 in `bare_metal::iommu::pt_alloc::tests::*` (`new_registry_is_empty`, `provision_allocates_and_records`, `provision_returns_distinct_roots_per_domain`, `provision_rejects_double_provision`, `provision_surfaces_frame_alloc_failure`, `provision_rejects_misaligned_frame_and_returns_it`, `release_drops_entry_and_frees_frame`, `release_unknown_domain_returns_not_provisioned`, `release_does_not_free_other_domain_root`, `reprovision_after_release_returns_new_root`, `entries_preserves_insertion_order_until_release`, `pt_page_bytes_is_4096`, `provisioned_count_tracks_alloc_and_release`); 6 in `bare_metal::iommu::tests::*` (`iommu_provision_domain_pt_passthrough_returns_zero_sentinel`, `iommu_provision_domain_pt_intel_round_trip`, `iommu_provision_domain_pt_amd_round_trip`, `iommu_provision_domain_pt_intel_rejects_double_provision`, `iommu_release_domain_pt_intel_rejects_unknown_domain`, `iommu_provision_domain_pt_surfaces_frame_alloc_failure`). Pure-state vendor-neutral allocator — zero MMIO bytes emitted. The live `install_*_device_entry` paths will consume `iommu_domain_pt_root_phys(domain)` once P6.7.9-pre.10 wires `DriverLoad` to call them after the PCI bind. **Predecessor (doc-lagged): P6.7.9-pre.8 IOMMU per-device driver bind landed 2026-05-22** (commit `84e183c` — `iommu::pci_bdfs_from_resources(&[Resource]) -> Vec<PciBdf>` extracts the BDFs from a manifest's `pci_devices` table, `driver_load` handler binds every extracted BDF via `iommu_install_domain` + `iommu_attach_device`, `ProcessControlBlock.bound_pci_devices: Vec<PciBdf>` records the bindings, `task_exit` calls `driver_load_handlers::tear_down_pci_bindings` to drain the PCB list and detach every BDF from the live IOMMU backend, +6 tests, doc-update pending — folded into this entry). **Predecessor: P6.7.9-pre.7 IOMMU per-device attach surface landed 2026-05-21**. (1) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/mod.rs`** introduces the vendor-neutral `PciBdf(u16)` newtype packing PCI bus/device/function in the canonical 16-bit form consumed by both VT-d source-id (high 8 bits = bus, low 8 bits = devfn) and AMD-Vi DeviceID (full 16 bits). Constructors `from_parts(bus, device, function)` (with explicit 5-bit / 3-bit masking on the device/function fields) + `from_raw(raw)`; accessors `raw()` / `bus()` / `devfn()` / `device()` / `function()`. (2) **`IommuBackend` trait extended** with `attach_device(bdf, domain) -> Result<(), IommuError>` + `detach_device(bdf) -> Result<(), IommuError>` — host-testable bookkeeping surface that records the binding without touching MMIO. `PassthroughBackend` returns `Ok(())` for both (no per-device state); `VtdBackend` + `AmdViBackend` track attachments in internal `Vec<{Vtd,AmdVi}Attachment>` with duplicate-attach → `IommuError::Unsupported` and detach-on-unknown → `IommuError::Unsupported`. `IommuKind::{Passthrough/Intel/Amd}` dispatches both methods through the static-dispatch match arms. Module-level `iommu_attach_device(bdf, domain)` / `iommu_detach_device(bdf)` close the public surface. (3) **Per-domain invalidation encoders**: new `INV_DESC_CTX_GRAN_DOMAIN = 0b10 << 4` + `INV_DESC_IOTLB_GRAN_DOMAIN = 0b10 << 4` constants (Intel VT-d spec § 6.5.2 G=10 selector); `encode_context_cache_domain_invalidate(domain) -> (u64, u64)` packing Type `0x1` + G `10` + DID in bits 16..31; `encode_iotlb_domain_invalidate(domain) -> (u64, u64)` packing Type `0x2` + G `10` + DID; AMD-Vi sibling `encode_invalidate_iommu_pages_domain(domain) -> (u64, u64)` packing opcode `0x3` + DID in bits 32..47 + S=1 spans-all in the high qword (spec § 5.4.4). (4) **Offset helpers**: `vtd::context_entry_offset(bdf) = devfn * CONTEXT_ENTRY_BYTES (16)` + `vtd::root_entry_offset(bus) = bus * ROOT_ENTRY_BYTES (16)` (both bounded to the 4-KiB per-page footprint); `amdvi::dte_offset(bdf) = bdf.raw() * DEVICE_TABLE_ENTRY_BYTES (32)` (bounds-checked against `DEVICE_TABLE_BYTES = 4096` for the Phase-1 1-frame device table). (5) **VT-d live install** (`#[cfg(target_os = "none")] VtdBackend::install_device_entry(phys_offset, bdf, domain, slpt_phys, context_table_phys, AddressWidth, TranslationType) -> Result<(), VtdAttachError>`): validates inputs (`hardware_activated`, 4-KiB alignment of `slpt_phys` / `context_table_phys`, domain installed, bdf not already attached), encodes the context entry via `encode_context_entry`, writes it into the per-bus context-table page via new `write_context_entry_at(context_va, ctx_offset, low, high)` helper, encodes the root entry via `encode_root_entry(context_table_phys)`, writes it into the global root-table page via new `write_root_entry_at(root_va, root_offset, low, high)` helper, submits the per-domain context-cache invalidate + per-domain IOTLB invalidate descriptors on the invalidation queue via new `submit_iq_descriptor(queue_va, unit_va, lo, hi) -> Result<(), ()>` helper (wraps on `INV_QUEUE_BYTES`; advances `IQT`; polls `IQH` to drain), records the attachment in `self.attachments`. (6) **AMD-Vi live install** (`#[cfg(target_os = "none")] AmdViBackend::install_device_entry(phys_offset, bdf, domain, iopt_phys, IommuFlags, PageMode) -> Result<(), AmdViAttachError>`): validates inputs (`hardware_activated`, 4-KiB alignment of `iopt_phys`, domain installed, bdf not already attached, mode != `NoTranslation`, DTE offset fits in `DEVICE_TABLE_BYTES`), encodes the DTE via `encode_device_table_entry`, writes it into the device table via new `write_dte_at(dev_table_va, byte_offset, qwords)` helper (4 sequential 64-bit volatile writes), submits `INVALIDATE_DEVTAB_ENTRY(device_id=bdf.raw())` + `INVALIDATE_IOMMU_PAGES(domain)` on the command buffer via new `submit_cmd_descriptor(buf_va, unit_va, lo, hi) -> Result<(), ()>` helper (wraps on `CMD_BUFFER_BYTES`; advances `CMD_BUFFER_TAIL`; polls `CMD_BUFFER_HEAD`). (7) **Error taxonomies**: `VtdAttachError` (5 variants: `NotActivated/DomainNotInstalled/AlreadyAttached/AddressMisaligned/InvalidationTimeout` → mapped to `IommuError::{ActivationFailed/InvalidDomain/Unsupported/AddressMisaligned/ActivationFailed}`); `AmdViAttachError` (7 variants: same 4 + `DeviceTableTooSmall/UnsupportedMode/InvalidationTimeout` → `IommuError::{ActivationFailed/InvalidDomain/Unsupported/AddressMisaligned/DomainTableFull/Unsupported/ActivationFailed}`); both via `From` impls. (8) **Module-level live wrappers** (`#[cfg(target_os = "none")]`): `install_vt_d_device_entry(phys_offset, bdf, domain, slpt_phys, context_table_phys, width, translation) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` + `install_amd_vi_device_entry(phys_offset, bdf, domain, iopt_phys, flags, mode) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` — both return `Ok(false)` when the live backend is the wrong vendor (no-op), `Ok(true)` on success, propagate errors via `IommuError::from`. Symmetric to the existing `activate_intel_vt_d` / `activate_amd_vi` pair. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-21 (**P6.7.9-pre.6 CLOSED — AMD-Vi live MMIO register programming wired per TASK-010 of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (1) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/amdvi.rs`** extended with the live-programming surface that closes the AMD half of TASK-010: 5 new STATUS status-mirror bit constants (`STATUS_BIT_EVENT_OVERFLOW=1<<0`, `STATUS_BIT_EVENT_LOG_INT=1<<1`, `STATUS_BIT_COM_WAIT_INT=1<<2`, `STATUS_BIT_EVENT_LOG_RUN=1<<3`, `STATUS_BIT_CMD_BUF_RUN=1<<4` per AMD IOMMU spec rev 3.10 § 5.5.4); 4 command-buffer layout constants (`CMD_BUFFER_ENTRY_BYTES=16`, `CMD_BUFFER_ENTRY_COUNT=256`, `CMD_BUFFER_BYTES=4096`, `CMD_BUFFER_LENGTH_ENCODING=8` per § 5.5.2); 4 event-log layout constants (mirror shape `EVENT_LOG_*`); 1 device-table size constant (`DEVICE_TABLE_SIZE_ENCODING=0` for 1-frame table per § 5.5.1); 5 command opcode constants (`CMD_OPCODE_COMPLETION_WAIT=0x1`, `CMD_OPCODE_INVALIDATE_DEVTAB=0x2`, `CMD_OPCODE_INVALIDATE_IOMMU_PAGES=0x3`, `CMD_OPCODE_INVALIDATE_IOTLB_PAGES=0x4`, `CMD_OPCODE_INVALIDATE_ALL=0x8` per § 5.4); `AMDVI_ACTIVATION_POLL_LIMIT=1_000_000` bounded retry budget. (2) **Pure-function encoders**: `encode_device_table_base(table_phys, size) -> u64` (bits 12..51 base masked, bits 0..8 Size); `encode_command_buffer_base(buf_phys, com_len) -> u64` (bits 12..51 base, bits 56..59 ComLen); `encode_event_log_base(log_phys, event_len) -> u64` (identical shape to command buffer); `encode_invalidate_devtab_entry(device_id) -> (u64, u64)` (lo qword bits 0..15 = DeviceID, bits 60..63 = opcode 0x2, hi qword = 0 per § 5.4.3). (3) **`AmdViBackend` state expansion**: 6 new fields (`unit_base: u64`, `device_table_phys: u64`, `command_buffer_phys: u64`, `event_log_phys: u64`, `command_buffer_tail: u64`, `hardware_activated: bool` — all `0`/`false` while dormant); 5 new `const fn` accessors (`unit_base()`, `device_table_phys()`, `command_buffer_phys()`, `event_log_phys()`, `is_hardware_activated()`); `prepare_activation(unit_base, device_table_phys, command_buffer_phys, event_log_phys)` pure-state update (idempotent for same params; clears `hardware_activated` when params change); new `AmdViActivateError` taxonomy (4 variants: `NotPrepared`, `CmdBufStartTimeout`, `EventLogStartTimeout`, `InvalidationTimeout`) with `impl From<AmdViActivateError> for IommuError → IommuError::ActivationFailed`. (4) **Live MMIO sequence** in `#[cfg(target_os = "none")] pub unsafe fn activate_hardware(&mut self, phys_offset: u64) -> Result<(), AmdViActivateError>`: spec-faithful six-step programming per AMD IOMMU § 5.3 + § 5.5: (a) `volatile_write64` `DEV_TAB_BAR ← encode_device_table_base(device_table_phys, 0)`; (b) `volatile_write64` `CMD_BUF_BASE ← encode_command_buffer_base(command_buffer_phys, 8)`; (c) `volatile_write64` `EVENT_LOG_BASE ← encode_event_log_base(event_log_phys, 8)`; (d) zero CMD/EVENT Head & Tail registers; (e) `volatile_write64` `CTRL ← CmdBufEn|EventLogEn`, bounded poll on `STATUS.CmdBufRun` then `STATUS.EventLogRun` (up to `AMDVI_ACTIVATION_POLL_LIMIT` iterations each with `core::hint::spin_loop`); (f) `write_cmd_entry(slot=0, encode_invalidate_devtab_entry(0))` + `volatile_write64` `CMD_BUFFER_TAIL ← 16` + bounded poll on `CMD_BUFFER_HEAD` reaching tail. `CTRL.IommuEn` is **NOT** raised by this slice — per-device translation gating lands when the driver framework attaches its first PCI device (future P6.7.9-pre.7+); until then the IOMMU stays in pre-translation pass-through at hardware level, preserving observable behaviour. New `unsafe fn mmio_read64/mmio_write64` helpers + `poll_status_bit(unit_va, bit)` + `poll_cmd_head_reaches(unit_va, tail)` + `write_cmd_entry(buf_va, slot, lo, hi)` — all `#[cfg(target_os = "none")]` gated, all using `core::ptr::{read_volatile, write_volatile}` exclusively. AMD-Vi register surface is uniformly 64-bit wide for the activation path, so 32-bit MMIO helpers (present in VT-d for GCMD/GSTS) are NOT wired here. (5) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/mod.rs`** extended: new `pub fn prepare_amd_vi_unit(unit_base, device_table_phys, command_buffer_phys, event_log_phys) -> Result<(), IommuError>` (routes through `with_iommu_backend` to the AMD variant, returns `Unsupported` for Passthrough/Intel — defence-in-depth); new `#[cfg(target_os = "none")] pub unsafe fn activate_amd_vi(phys_offset: u64) -> Result<bool, IommuError>` (returns `Ok(false)` when not AMD or `iommu_unit_base() == 0`); `iommu_hardware_activated()` extended to dispatch through the AMD variant (was Intel-only). (6) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/lib.rs` kmain extended**: after the existing P6.7.9-pre.5 VT-d block and before scheduler init, a new `#[cfg(all(target_arch = "x86_64", target_os = "none"))]` block fires only when `iommu_unit_base() != 0 && iommu_vendor() == Amd`. It allocates three frames from `FRAME_ALLOC` (device-table + command-buffer + event-log), zero-fills them via the bootloader direct-map (`core::ptr::write_bytes`), calls `prepare_amd_vi_unit` + `activate_amd_vi(phys_offset_mb2)`, then logs one of `[iommu] amd-vi activated  unit=<base>` (Ok(true) — AMD-Vi live MMIO completed), `[iommu] amd-vi activate skip` (Ok(false) — passthrough/Intel), `[iommu] amd-vi activate err` (any `IommuError`), `[iommu] amd-vi prepare err`, or `[iommu] amd-vi alloc err` — single-line surface for the QEMU + Proxmox boot smoke. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-21 (**P6.7.9-pre.4 CLOSED — DMA-Map vendor switch wired per TASK-010 of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (1) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/mod.rs`** extended with a new vendor-dispatch surface: `pub enum IommuKind { Passthrough(PassthroughBackend), Intel(vtd::VtdBackend), Amd(amdvi::AmdViBackend) }` that implements `IommuBackend` via static-dispatch match arms (no `dyn` indirection, no allocator overhead beyond the inner backend's owned `Vec`s). `IommuKind::new_passthrough() -> Self` is `const fn` so the kernel-wide `pub static IOMMU_BACKEND: spin::Mutex<IommuKind>` static initialises at static-init time. New `pub fn install_backend_for_vendor(vendor: IommuVendor)` swaps the live variant — called exactly once from `kmain` after `iommu::probe` resolves the firmware vendor. New `pub fn with_iommu_backend<R>(f: impl FnOnce(&mut IommuKind) -> R) -> R` brackets the mutex around a closure receiving `&mut IommuKind`, which implements `IommuBackend` so all trait methods are callable through it. New `pub const fn domain_for_task(task_id: u64) -> DomainId` projects the kernel `TaskId` into the 16-bit VT-d `DID` / AMD-Vi `DomainID` space (Phase 1 one-domain-per-process model per OIP-013 § S3.5). (2) **`VtdBackend::new()` and `AmdViBackend::new()` promoted to `pub const fn`** in `iommu/vtd.rs` and `iommu/amdvi.rs` so the static can hold the variants without lazy `OnceLock` overhead — `alloc::vec::Vec::new()` has been `const` since Rust 1.39 and works under the workspace edition 2024 pin. (3) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/lib.rs` kmain extended**: after the existing `iommu::set_iommu_vendor(probe.vendor)` + `iommu::set_iommu_unit_count(unit_count)` writes, `kmain` now calls `iommu::install_backend_for_vendor(probe.vendor)` to swap the live `IOMMU_BACKEND` variant in line with the firmware advertisement. The `[iommu] vendor=<intel|amd|passthrough> units=N` boot-log line is emitted after the swap, unchanged. (4) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs::dma_map_handlers` refactored**: imports `IommuBackend`, `IommuFlags`, `domain_for_task`, `with_iommu_backend` from `crate::bare_metal::iommu`. In `dma_map(args)`: after the cap-token verification and the duplicate-iova-base check, derives `let domain_id = domain_for_task(current.0)` and calls `with_iommu_backend(|b| b.install_domain(domain_id))` (idempotent — backend keeps the domain across repeat `DmaMap` invocations from the same process; returns `ENOSPC` on backend error). After the contiguous-frame install completes, the handler calls `with_iommu_backend(|b| { let res = b.map(domain_id, iova_base, phys_base, len, map_flags); if res.is_ok() { let _ = b.flush(domain_id); } res })` with `map_flags` derived from the `direction` syscall arg (`0→IommuFlags::READ`, `1→IommuFlags::WRITE`, default `READ|WRITE`); backend `map` failure triggers a full PT rollback (unmap every installed page, return every frame to the allocator) and returns `ENOSPC`. (5) **`tear_down_dma_mappings(task)` extended**: derives `let domain_id = domain_for_task(task.0)` and for every `DmaMapping` on the PCB calls `with_iommu_backend(|b| { let r = b.unmap(domain_id, m.iova_base, bytes); let _ = b.flush(domain_id); r })` — errors swallowed because `UnmapFailed` is benign for teardown when `dma_map` previously rolled back. PT teardown logic preserved verbatim (resolve phys before unmap + return frame to allocator + invlpg per page). (6) **Build Info panel** (`crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/demo.rs::render_buildinfo`): Active=`P6.7.9-pre.4 DMA-Map vendor switch` (cyan), Next=`P6.7.9-pre.5 IOMMU register programming`, Phase=`1 - Microkernel POC  (~99.9%)`, Tests=`1078 workspace pass`. Workspace test count 1064 → **1078 pass / 0 fail** (`cargo test --workspace --all-features -- --test-threads=1`). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-21 (**P6.7.9-pre.2 CLOSED — Intel VT-d backend scaffold landed dormant per TASK-010 of `docs/planning/2026-05-21-development-plan.md`**). (1) **New module** `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/vtd.rs` (~1060 lines): pure-data slice of the Intel VT-d second-level translation backend that will eventually replace `super::PassthroughBackend` when `iommu_vendor()` reports `IommuVendor::Intel`. The slice lands **register offsets + data-structure encoders + a host-testable dormant backend**; the live MMIO programming is deferred to P6.7.9-pre.4 (DMA-Map vendor switch). (2) **Register-offset surface** (`pub const u32` per Intel VT-d spec rev 4.1 § 10.4): `REG_OFFSET_VER=0x00`, `REG_OFFSET_CAP=0x08`, `REG_OFFSET_ECAP=0x10`, `REG_OFFSET_GCMD=0x18`, `REG_OFFSET_GSTS=0x1C`, `REG_OFFSET_RTADDR=0x20`, `REG_OFFSET_CCMD=0x28`, `REG_OFFSET_FSTS=0x34`, `REG_OFFSET_FECTL=0x38`, `REG_OFFSET_FEDATA=0x3C`, `REG_OFFSET_FEADDR=0x40`, `REG_OFFSET_FEUADDR=0x44`, `REG_OFFSET_PMEN=0x64`, `REG_OFFSET_IQH=0x80`, `REG_OFFSET_IQT=0x88`, `REG_OFFSET_IQA=0x90`. GCMD/GSTS bit positions: `GCMD_BIT_TE=1<<31`, `GCMD_BIT_SRTP=1<<30`, `GCMD_BIT_SFL=1<<29`, `GCMD_BIT_EAFL=1<<28`, `GCMD_BIT_WBF=1<<27`, `GCMD_BIT_QIE=1<<26`, `GCMD_BIT_IRE=1<<25`, `GCMD_BIT_SIRTP=1<<24`, `GCMD_BIT_CFI=1<<23`. (3) **Data-structure encoders** (Intel VT-d spec § 9): `RootEntry { low, high }` 128-bit + `encode_root_entry(ctp_phys) -> Result<RootEntry, VtdError>` setting bit 0 (Present) + bits 12..63 (CTP); `encode_root_entry_absent() -> RootEntry` for clean-state initialization. `ContextEntry { low, high }` 128-bit + `encode_context_entry(slpt_phys, domain, translation, width) -> Result<ContextEntry, VtdError>` encoding bit 0 (P), bits 2..3 (T), bits 12..63 (SLPTPTR) in `low` and bits 0..2 (AW), bits 8..23 (DID) in `high`; `encode_context_entry_absent()` for not-present entries. `Slpte(u64)` second-level page-table entry + `encode_slpte(phys, IommuFlags) -> Result<Slpte, VtdError>` translating kernel `IommuFlags::{READ, WRITE, EXECUTE, COHERENT}` into VT-d `R/W/X/SNP` bits (write-only entries auto-promoted to RW per VT-d malformed-entry semantics, output_address mask `0x000F_FFFF_FFFF_F000`). (4) **Two `pub` enums**: `TranslationType::{UntranslatedOnly=0b00, UntranslatedAndTranslated=0b01, Passthrough=0b10}` and `AddressWidth::{Bits30Level2=0, Bits39Level3=1, Bits48Level4=2, Bits57Level5=3}` with `levels() -> u8` accessor returning 2/3/4/5 paging levels. (5) **CAP register decoders** (pure functions): `cap_domain_count(cap) -> u32` returns `1 << (4 + 2 * ND)` saturated to 65_536 for the 16-bit DID space (validated for ND=0..7 — 16/64/256/1024/4096/16384/65536/65536). `cap_supported_agaw(cap) -> u8` extracts SAGAW bits 8..12 as a 5-bit mask. `cap_caching_mode(cap) -> bool` extracts bit 7. `pick_highest_supported_agaw(mask) -> Option<AddressWidth>` prefers `Bits57Level5 → Bits48Level4 → Bits39Level3 → Bits30Level2 → None`. (6) **Host-testable `VtdBackend`**: `struct { domains: Vec<DomainId>, mappings: Vec<ScaffoldMapping> }` + `impl IommuBackend` with `vendor() = IommuVendor::Intel`, idempotent `install_domain`, `map` validating known-domain + 4-KiB alignment + encoding leaf SL-PTE via `encode_slpte` + pushing a `ScaffoldMapping` record, `unmap` retaining matching mappings and erroring `UnmapFailed` on no-match, `flush` validating known-domain only. **Emits zero MMIO bytes** — the live `unsafe` register programming + queued-invalidation descriptor write lands in P6.7.9-pre.4. `ScaffoldMapping { domain, iova, phys, len, leaf_slpte }` is `pub` so the host test suite can introspect the recorded state. `VtdError::{AddressMisaligned, UnknownDomain, UnsupportedFlags}` taxonomy + `impl From<VtdError> for IommuError` maps to `IommuError::{AddressMisaligned, InvalidDomain, Unsupported}`. (7) **Module registration**: `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/iommu/mod.rs` extended with `pub mod vtd;` (4 submodules now: `dmar`, `domain`, `ivrs`, `vtd`). No new dependency: pure `core` + `alloc::vec::Vec`. (4) **Live wiring of the 3 driver-image siblings** (`crates/omni-driver-{net-virtio,nvme,e1000e}-image/`): each `Cargo.toml` extended with `omni-driver-shared = { path = "../omni-driver-shared" }` path dependency (no version pin — same-repo; zero new transitive deps). Each `src/main.rs` rewritten: `#[allow(dead_code)]` gates removed from `syscall5`, `SYS_MMIO_MAP`, `SYS_DMA_MAP`, `SYS_IRQ_ATTACH` (all four symbols now live). The `_start` `extern "C" fn` now (a) retrieves three tokens via `find_token(ACTION_TAG_MMIO_MAP, |_| true)` + `find_token(ACTION_TAG_DMA_MAP, |_| true)` + `find_token(ACTION_TAG_IRQ_ATTACH, |_| true)`, (b) issues `syscall5(SYS_MMIO_MAP, phys_base, len, flags=0, token.as_ptr() as u64, token.len() as u64)` against the manifest-pinned BAR (virtio-net `VIRTIO_BAR4_PHYS_BASE = 0xFEBC_0000` / `VIRTIO_BAR4_LEN = 0x1000`; NVMe `NVME_BAR0_PHYS_BASE = 0xFEBF_0000` / `NVME_BAR0_LEN = 0x4000`; e1000e `E1000E_BAR0_PHYS_BASE = 0xFEB0_0000` / `E1000E_BAR0_LEN = 0x20000`), (c) issues `syscall5(SYS_DMA_MAP, DMA_IOVA_BASE = 0x0, DMA_LEN_4_GIB = 0x1_0000_0000, DMA_DIR_BIDIR = 2, token.as_ptr(), token.len())`, (d) issues `syscall5(SYS_IRQ_ATTACH, IRQ_LINE = 33/34/35, IPC_CHANNEL_PLACEHOLDER = 0, token.as_ptr(), token.len(), 0)` (ABI: 4 args, a4 unused), (e) only on `errno = 0` from all three syscalls advances the `BringUp` FSM through its remaining pure-state phases via repeated `Event::Advance` until terminal (`Phase::DriverOk` for virtio-net; `Phase::Ready` for NVMe and e1000e). Sentinel exit codes (`EXIT_OK=0`, `EXIT_FSM_FAILED=1`, `EXIT_NO_MMIO_TOKEN=10`, `EXIT_NO_DMA_TOKEN=20`, `EXIT_NO_IRQ_TOKEN=30`, `EXIT_MMIO_BASE=40`, `EXIT_DMA_BASE=60`, `EXIT_IRQ_BASE=80`) distinguish standalone execution (no DriverLoad — sentinel 10/20/30) from loader-rejected tokens (sentinel 40+errno / 60+errno / 80+errno). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-20 (**P6.7.8.9 CLOSED — capability deposit trampoline wired end-to-end per OIP-013 § S5.3 step 8**). (1) **Tre nuovi moduli kernel**: (a) `crates/omni-kernel/src/entropy.rs` — Phase-1 CSPRNG con `seed_from_hw_32()` (mix `RDRAND` cpuid-gated 10-retry + `RDTSC` jitter + SplitMix64 finalizer su 4 chunk a 64-bit) e `KernelCsprng` wrapper su `ChaCha20Rng` da `rand_chacha 0.3`; global `static KERNEL_CSPRNG: spin::Mutex<Option<KernelCsprng>>` con lazy init via `with_csprng(|rng| …)` accessor; Phase-2 API `add_entropy(&[u8])` (XOR-mix nel buffer corrente + reseed) + `reseed([u8;32])` (full re-key) **designed ma not wired** — i call site Phase-2 (IRQ handler chain, network driver post-bringup) restano follow-up. (b) `crates/omni-kernel/src/driver_cap_issuer.rs` — kernel-side Ed25519 signing key statica `DRIVER_CAP_ISSUER_SEED = [0xCAFEBABE × 8]` (DEV ONLY placeholder, sostituzione TEE-derived sealing key deferita a P5.2 + OIP key-custody policy); helper `kernel_signing_key()` produce un `OmniSigningKey::from_bytes`. (c) `crates/omni-kernel/src/cap_deposit.rs` — wire-format header `OMNICAPS` magic + version 1 + entry count + flat indexed entry table `[u32 action_tag, u32 resource_tag, u32 token_offset, u32 token_len]` × N + packed postcard `CapabilityToken` blobs; mappato read-only (`PTE_PRESENT|PTE_USER|PTE_NO_EXEC`) a `DRIVER_CAP_DEPOSIT_VA = 0x0000_0000_0010_0000` (1 MiB) per `DRIVER_CAP_DEPOSIT_PAGES = 8` pagine = `DRIVER_CAP_DEPOSIT_LEN = 0x8000` (32 KiB, sized per worst-case 64 entry × ~150 byte/token postcard + header); encoder `encode_deposit_page` mintà un `CapabilityToken` per ogni `Resource` in `DriverCapabilities` (`mmio_regions → MmioMap`, `dma_windows → DmaMap`, `irq_lines → IrqAttach`, `pci_devices → PciConfigRead+PciConfigWrite`) con `CapabilityId::from_bytes(KERNEL_CSPRNG.next_16_bytes())` (bypass `omni-capability/mint` feature evitando `getrandom`/`id-generation` su bare-metal — `CapabilityId::from_bytes` è `pub const fn` non-feature-gated, `CapabilityToken::sign_payload` è unconditional) + `subject = NodeId::from_attestation_hash(provider.node_id_bytes())` (placeholder `[0u8; 32]` finché P5.2 non integra TEE-attested node id) + `TimeWindow { not_before: rtc_seconds(), not_after: + DEPOSIT_TOKEN_LIFETIME_SECONDS }` (90 giorni) + signed via `CapabilityToken::sign_payload(&kernel_key, payload)`; bare-metal `deposit_for_driver` alloca + mappa 8 frame contigui via `address_space.map_user_4k` + popola via `core::ptr::copy_nonoverlapping` attraverso il direct-map. (2) **Wiring in `driver_load_handlers::driver_load`**: dopo `spawn_from_elf` ritorna `Ok(task_id)`, il handler legge il PCB del driver via `sched.process_mut(task_id)`, costruisce un `PageMapper` con il `BOOT_CR3`, e chiama `cap_deposit::deposit_for_driver(&manifest.capabilities, boot_seconds, subject_node, &address_space, &mut mapper, alloc)`. Su success registra `pcb.cap_deposit_va = Some(va)`; su failure il `task_id` viene comunque ritornato (driver vive senza capability — primo `MmioMap` → `EACCES` osservabile in user space; future P6.7.8.10 wires `scheduler.cancel_spawn` per rollback atomico). (3) **`ProcessControlBlock` esteso** con `cap_deposit_va: Option<u64>` (`None` per processi senza deposit, e.g. mb11/mb12 userprobe). `Ed25519CapabilityProvider::node_id_bytes()` `pub const fn` accessor aggiunto. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-20 (**P6.7.8.8 CLOSED — `DriverLoad (73)` syscall handler wired end-to-end per OIP-013 § S5.3**). (1) **Nuovo modulo `driver_load_handlers`** in `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs` (`#[cfg(all(feature = "bare-metal", target_os = "none", not(test)))]`), specchiato sul pattern P6.7.8.1 / P6.7.8.3 (`mmio_map_handlers`, `dma_map_handlers`, `irq_attach_handlers`). Espone `pub(super) fn driver_load(args: [u64; 6]) -> SyscallReturn` con ABI: `a1 = pack_ptr` (omni-pack v1 blob, user VA), `a2 = pack_len` (≤ `MAX_PACK_BYTES = 32 MiB`), `a3 = cap_ptr` (postcard `CapabilityToken`), `a4 = cap_len` (≤ `MAX_TOKEN_BYTES = 1024`). Sequenza di check OIP-013 § S5.3: (a) EFAULT su cap_ptr=0/cap_len=0/cap_len>1024/cap range fuori user-half; (b) EFAULT su pack_ptr=0, EINVAL su pack_len=0/pack_len>32 MiB, EFAULT su pack range fuori user-half; (c) copia token in stack buffer `[u8; 1024]` via `core::ptr::copy_nonoverlapping`; (d) `verify_token(token_bytes)` = postcard `decode_canonical::<CapabilityToken>` + `Ed25519CapabilityProvider::placeholder().verify_signed_token` + `is_driver_framework_action(action) && action == Action::DriverLoad` + `resource == Resource::Any` (defence-in-depth: un token scoped a un singolo PciDevice non basta); (e) alloca `Vec<u8>` di `pack_len_usize` byte sull'heap bump + `copy_nonoverlapping` user→kernel; (f) `decode_omni_pack(&pack_buf)` (header magic + version + flags=0 + sezioni disjoint/contained, signature_len=64) + `postcard_decode_manifest(sections.manifest)` (no-trailing-bytes invariant da `OIP-Serde-004`) + `hydrate_manifest(body, *sections.signature)`; (g) `verify_manifest(&manifest, sections.image)` chain BLAKE3-hash + KNOWN_ISSUERS lookup + Ed25519 verify contro `encode_canonical(&body)`; (h) `manifest_errno` mapping (`MalformedPack`/`PackTooLarge`/`ImageHashMismatch` → `EINVAL`, `UnknownIssuer`/`SignatureInvalid` → `EACCES`); (i) `ProcessControlBlock::spawn_from_elf(sections.image, PhysAddr(boot_pml4), &mut mapper, alloc, sched, PriorityClass::System, KernelPrincipal::ZERO)`; (j) ritorno `SyscallReturn::ok(task_id.0)` su successo, `SyscallReturn::err(ENOSPC)` su spawn failure. (2) **Nuovo `bare_metal::BOOT_CR3` static** (`core::sync::atomic::AtomicU64`) con `set_boot_cr3(value)` (low-12-bit mask defensive — accetta raw CR3 con PCD/PWT/PCID flag sotto la PML4 base alignata) e `boot_cr3()` accessor `Relaxed`. Mirror simmetrico a `PHYS_OFFSET`. Wirato in `kmain` subito dopo `let cr3_raw = arch::read_cr3();`. Lo handler legge `boot_cr3()` per passare la boot PML4 come `boot_cr3` parameter a `spawn_from_elf` — la CR3 attiva nel syscall è quella del loader, non del kernel image; il clone della kernel-half DEVE avvenire contro la boot PML4. (3) **Dispatcher wiring** in `KernelSyscallDispatcher`: `SyscallNumber::DriverLoad` spostato dal `NotYetImplemented` tail arm al `MmioMap | DmaMap | IrqAttach | DriverLoad` legacy arm (returns `CapabilityDenied` defensive sentinel); `dispatch_full` nuovo arm `DriverLoad` route a `driver_load_handlers::driver_load(args)` su bare-metal o `SyscallReturn::err(EACCES)` su host build. (4) **Host-side test refactor**: `dispatcher_remaining_driver_framework_syscalls_return_not_yet_implemented` (3 syscall) → `dispatcher_remaining_tee_syscalls_return_not_yet_implemented` (2 syscall — DriverLoad rimosso); `dispatcher_driver_framework_legacy_arm_returns_capability_denied` esteso con DriverLoad (3→4); `dispatcher_full_dma_map_and_irq_attach_surface_eaccess_on_host` → `dispatcher_full_dma_map_irq_attach_and_driver_load_surface_eaccess_on_host` (2→3); `kernel_syscall_dispatch_driver_framework_numbers_route` range `(70..=72)` → `(70..=73)`. (5) **+3 nuovi host-side test** `bare_metal::boot_cr3_tests::*` (`set_boot_cr3_masks_low_12_bits` + `boot_cr3_returns_zero_when_unset_observer` + `set_boot_cr3_round_trips_aligned_value`) — snapshottano e ripristinano il global per non perturbare gli altri host test. Test pinning ogni byte value + 4 rejection paths (ixgbe 82599, X550, virtio-net Red Hat, Realtek RTL8169, all-zero triple). (3) **Modulo `controller_regs`** (10 host-side test, split into device-control / RX-ring / TX-ring / MAC blocks per cognitive-complexity ≤ 20) — Intel 82574L datasheet § 10.2-10.8 CSR offsets pinned: device control (`CTRL=0x0000`, `STATUS=0x0008`); PHY/MDIO (`MDIC=0x0020`); interrupts (`ICR=0x00C0`, `ITR=0x00C4`, `IMS=0x00D0`, `IMC=0x00D8`); RX ring (`RCTL=0x0100`, `RDBAL=0x2800`, `RDBAH=0x2804`, `RDLEN=0x2808`, `RDH=0x2810`, `RDT=0x2818`); TX ring (`TCTL=0x0400`, `TDBAL=0x3800`, `TDBAH=0x3804`, `TDLEN=0x3808`, `TDH=0x3810`, `TDT=0x3818`); MAC (`RAL0=0x5400`, `RAH0=0x5404`). Field encodings: `CTRL_RST_BIT=1<<26` (global reset), `STATUS_FD_BIT=1<<0` / `STATUS_LU_BIT=1<<1` (full-duplex / link-up); `IMC_DISABLE_ALL=0xFFFFFFFF` (sentinel for bring-up step 2); `RCTL_EN_BIT=1<<1` / `RCTL_BAM_BIT=1<<15` / `RCTL_SECRC_BIT=1<<26` / `RCTL_BSIZE_SHIFT=16` (BSIZE=0b00 = 2 KiB); `TCTL_EN_BIT=1<<1` / `TCTL_PSP_BIT=1<<3` / `TCTL_CT_SHIFT=4` / `TCTL_COLD_SHIFT=12` / `TCTL_CT_DEFAULT=0x0F` (IEEE 802.3) / `TCTL_COLD_DEFAULT_FD=0x40` (full-duplex); `RAH_AV_BIT=1<<31` (Address Valid). `rctl_enable_value() -> u32` const-fn compone RCTL.EN | BAM | SECRC; `tctl_enable_value() -> u32` const-fn compone TCTL.EN | PSP | CT_DEFAULT << CT_SHIFT | COLD_DEFAULT_FD << COLD_SHIFT. `CSR_REGION_BYTES = 0x20000` (128 KiB MMIO window per OIP-015 § S5.1 step 1). Due `const _: () = assert!(...)` compile-time layout invariants (region cover RAH0 + TDT; TX block 0x1000 bytes past RX block) per evitare la `assert!(true)` lint via `clippy::assertions-on-constants`. (4) **Modulo `interrupts`** (7 host-side test) — `TXDW_BIT = 1<<0`, `LSC_BIT = 1<<2`, `RXT0_BIT = 1<<7` (Intel 82574L datasheet § 10.6.6 ICR layout); `ENABLED_IMS = RXT0|TXDW|LSC = 0x85` pinned a OIP-015 § S5.1 step 10 mandate. `icr_has_rx/has_tx/has_link_change(icr: u32) -> bool` const classifiers consumed by the kernel-installed IRQ trampoline + driver-side dispatch. Test pin bit positions, IMS literal value `0x0000_0085`, `count_ones()==3` invariant, per-bit classifier discrimination, burst-OR handling, unrelated-bit rejection. (5) **Modulo `ring_config`** (15 host-side test) — `MIN_RING_DEPTH=1`, `MAX_RING_DEPTH=4096`, `MIN_RX_BUFFER_COUNT=1`, `MAX_RX_BUFFER_COUNT=8192` per OIP-015 § S1.1; manifest defaults `DEFAULT_RX_RING_DEPTH=DEFAULT_TX_RING_DEPTH=256` / `DEFAULT_RX_BUFFER_COUNT=512`; descriptor sizes `RX_DESCRIPTOR_BYTES=TX_DESCRIPTOR_BYTES=16` (Intel 82574L datasheet § 10.7.1 / § 10.8.1 legacy format); `RX_BUFFER_BYTES=2048` (matches `RCTL.BSIZE=0b00`). Validators `is_valid_ring_depth(u32) -> bool` con power-of-two requirement per OIP-015 § S1.1 (hardware ring pointer wrap relies on `depth & (depth-1) == 0`); `is_valid_rx_buffer_count(u32) -> bool` count-only check; `rx_ring_bytes(u32) -> Option<usize>` / `tx_ring_bytes(u32) -> Option<usize>` con `checked_mul` defence-in-depth. Test su bounds match OIP, defaults match manifest, default-validation pass, descriptor-size pin, RX-buffer-size pin, validator-rejects-zero, rejects-above-max, rejects-non-pow2, accepts-every-pow2-in-bounds, rx-buffer-count rejection-paths + range coverage, byte-size pinning a 4 KiB (256 entries) e 64 KiB (max). (6) **Modulo `bringup`** (22 host-side test) — 13-step bring-up state machine per OIP-015 § S5.1 + § S8: `Phase` enum `#[repr(u8)]` (`PciEnumeration=0 → MmioMap=1 → DisableInterrupts=2 → GlobalReset=3 → ReadMac=4 → PhyInit=5 → SetupRxRing=6 → PostRxBuffers=7 → SetupTxRing=8 → ConfigureRxTx=9 → EnableInterrupts=10 → AttachIrq=11 → RegisterNetChannel=12 → Ready=13` + terminal `Failed=14`). `Phase::{next, is_terminal, is_live}` pure-function `const`. `BringUp { phase, retries: u8 }` state-machine driver con shape identica al precedent virtio-net P6.7.8.3 e NVMe P6.7.8.4: `Event::{Advance, Retry, Abort(BringUpError)}` + `MAX_RETRIES=3` + `BringUpError` (11 variants: `NoMatchingDevice`, `MmioMapFailed`, `ResetTimeout`, `InvalidMac`, `PhyInitFailed`, `DmaMapFailed`, `IrqAttachFailed`, `NetChannelRegistrationFailed`, `InvalidRingDepth`, `RetryBudgetExhausted`, `TerminalAdvanceAttempted`). `StepKind` projection (15 variants: `EnumeratePci`, `MapControllerRegisters`, `WriteImcMaskAll`, `TriggerCtrlReset`, `ReadReceiveAddress`, `IssueMdioAutonegotiate`, `AllocateRxRing`, `PrepostRxBuffers`, `AllocateTxRing`, `WriteRctlTctl`, `WriteImsEnabled`, `AttachMsiXVector`, `RegisterNetChannel`, `EnterRxTxLoop`, `ParkExit`). Le actual syscall invocations restano deferred al sibling image crate P6.7.8.7. **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-20 (**P6.7.8.3 CLOSED — virtio-net bring-up FSM + `DmaMap (71)` + `IrqAttach (72)` syscall handlers + bootable image sibling crate landed in single-shot**). (1) **`DmaMap (71)` syscall handler** wired end-to-end in `crates/omni-kernel/src/bare_metal/syscall_entry.rs::dma_map_handlers` per `OIP-Driver-Framework-013` § S3 con due-register ABI (rax=phys_base, rdx=errno): (a) input validation EINVAL su page alignment + reserved direction + reserved IOVA range (deve essere ⊂ `[0x0000_0100_0000_0000, 0x0000_0180_0000_0000)` 512 GiB driver-DMA PML4 slot, disjoint dal MMIO slot); (b) EFAULT su cap_ptr/cap_len out-of-user-half o cap_len > 1024; (c) copy postcard token su kernel stack buffer, `omni_types::wire::decode_canonical::<CapabilityToken>` + `Ed25519CapabilityProvider::verify_signed_token` + `is_driver_framework_action` + `Action::DmaMap` + `Resource::DmaWindow` subset-contains range check; (d) duplicate-iova rejection (EINVAL) sul PCB; (e) **Phase 1 no-IOMMU passthrough**: alloc contiguous frames da `FRAME_ALLOC` con strict-contiguity check (rollback su prima non-adjacent allocation; identity-mapped `iova == user_va == phys` 1:1 in caller AS); (f) map_user_4k con flags `PRESENT|WRITABLE|USER|NX` (DMA buffer non-eseguibile) + `invlpg` per page; (g) record `DmaMapping { iova_base, len_pages, direction }` sul PCB; (h) return `SyscallReturn::ok(phys_base)` (il valore che il driver scriverà nei DMA descriptor del device — senza IOMMU il device vede phys); (i) rollback page-by-page con `unmap_4k` + `free_frame` su qualunque map failure; (j) `tear_down_dma_mappings(task_id)` invocato in `task_exit` PRIMA di `sched.dequeue` (frame ritornano al FRAME_ALLOC; pcb.dma_mappings drained). I vendor backends IOMMU (`vtd` DMAR + `amdvi` IVRS) restano deferred a P6.7.8.x — il commento nel modulo lo documenta esplicitamente. (2) **`IrqAttach (72)` syscall handler** wired end-to-end in `irq_attach_handlers::irq_attach` per `OIP-Driver-Framework-013` § S4: (a) decode postcard `CapabilityToken` → `verify_signed_token` → `Action::IrqAttach` + `Resource::IrqLine` subset-contains; (b) shared-line rejection (linear scan dei 191 slot della tabella per-vettore; ritorna EINVAL come proxy per EBUSY — clean-up `EBUSY = 16` da aggiungere a `syscall_errno` in follow-up); (c) `allocate_vector` su bitmap `IRQ_VECTOR_BASE=0x40..=IRQ_VECTOR_END=0xFE` (190 vettori) tramite CAS-reservazione di `(irq_line, owner_task, channel_id)` su `AtomicU32`/`AtomicU64`; (d) channel-existence check via `crate::ipc::ipc_registry().channel(ChannelId(_))` (rifiuta canali destrutti); (e) install IDT trampoline (`idt_set_vector(vector, omni_irq_dispatch_trampoline)`); (f) record `IrqAttachment { irq_line, vector, channel_id }` sul PCB; (g) return `SyscallReturn::ok(vector as u64)` (il vettore allocato è il return-value primario). Nuovo asm `omni_irq_dispatch_trampoline` (`#[unsafe(no_mangle)]` + `global_asm!` con 9-push caller-saved + `call kernel_irq_dispatch_handler` + 9-pop + iretq; stack-aligned 16-byte verificato matematicamente nel commento). Rust-side `kernel_irq_dispatch_handler` chiama `lapic::read_in_service_vector` (nuovo helper che scansiona `ISR.B0..B7` MSR `0x810..=0x817` in x2APIC mode o MMIO `0x0100..=0x0170` step 16 in xAPIC, highest-bank-first per highest-priority winner per Intel SDM Vol 3A § 10.8.4) + `irq_attach_handlers::dispatch_fire(vector)` (incrementa `missed: AtomicU32` counter + `lapic_eoi`). `tear_down_irq_attachments(task_id)` invocato in `task_exit` rilascia gli slot. Real channel-enqueue (`IrqNotification::{Tick, MissedSince(u32)}` su omni.driver.* channel) resta deferred — il counter incrementa così la fire è osservabile via boot-time smoke. (3) **FSM bring-up estesa** in `crates/omni-driver-net-virtio/src/bringup.rs`: nuovo `BringUp { phase: Phase, retries: u8 }` state-machine driver + `Event::{Advance, Retry, Abort(BringUpError)}` + `BringUpError` (8 varianti pure-data: `DeviceFailed`, `RequiredFeaturesAbsent`, `FeaturesNotAccepted`, `MmioMapFailed`, `DmaMapFailed`, `IrqAttachFailed`, `RetryBudgetExhausted`, `TerminalAdvanceAttempted`) + `MAX_RETRIES = 3` retry budget (bound bring-up latency a 3 tentativi per fase) + `StepKind` proiezione descrittiva (7 varianti: `WriteDeviceStatus(u8)`, `NegotiateFeatures`, `ReadDeviceStatus`, `ConfigureVirtqueues`, `ReadMac`, `SetDriverOk`, `ParkExit`). `on_event` implementa: `Advance` → `phase.next()` + retry counter reset (errore se terminal phase); `Retry` → retry counter +1, transizione a `Failed` con `RetryBudgetExhausted` se raggiunge MAX_RETRIES; `Abort(err)` → transizione diretta a `Failed`. (4) **Modulo `device_status`** (3 host-side test) — bit constants da virtio 1.0 § 2.1 per il Common Configuration `device_status` byte: `RESET = 0x00`, `ACKNOWLEDGE = 0x01`, `DRIVER = 0x02`, `DRIVER_OK = 0x04`, `FEATURES_OK = 0x08`, `DEVICE_NEEDS_RESET = 0x40`, `FAILED = 0x80`. Test `reset_is_zero` (preserva il path § S4.1 step 2), `status_bits_are_disjoint` (per ogni coppia distinta, `a & b == 0` — prevenire la conflagrazione fra phase identifier), `fully_initialised_status_matches_spec` (`ACKNOWLEDGE | DRIVER | FEATURES_OK | DRIVER_OK == 0x0F` anchor). (5) **Modulo `features`** (4 host-side test) — `VIRTIO_F_VERSION_1 = 1u64 << 32` + `VIRTIO_NET_F_MAC = 1u64 << 5` + `VIRTIO_NET_F_STATUS = 1u64 << 16` come `REQUIRED_FEATURES` (mandatory floor OIP-015 § S4.1 step 4); `VIRTIO_NET_F_CSUM = 1u64 << 0` + `VIRTIO_NET_F_MRG_RXBUF = 1u64 << 15` opzionali (gated dal manifest `[net].tx_checksum_offload` / `[net].lro_enabled`). Test `version_1_lives_in_upper_bank` (bit ≥ 32 anchor per il bank-1 lookup virtio 1.0 § 6), `required_features_covers_mandatory_three`, `optional_csum_does_not_overlap_required`, `optional_mrg_rxbuf_does_not_overlap_required` (defence in depth contro doppia-allocazione di bit). (6) **Modulo `virtqueue`** (8 host-side test) — `RX_QUEUE_IDX = 0` / `TX_QUEUE_IDX = 1` (virtio-net § 5.1.2 pin), `DEFAULT_RX_QUEUE_DEPTH = DEFAULT_TX_QUEUE_DEPTH = 256` (OIP-015 § S1 default), `MAX_QUEUE_DEPTH = 4096` (OIP-015 § S1.1 ceiling), `VIRTQ_DESC_BYTES = 16` (virtio 1.0 § 2.4.5: `{u64 addr, u32 len, u16 flags, u16 next}`), `VIRTQ_AVAIL_FIXED_BYTES = 6`, `VIRTQ_USED_FIXED_BYTES = 6`, `VIRTQ_USED_ELEM_BYTES = 8`. Pure-function helper `is_valid_queue_depth(depth) -> bool` (power-of-2 in `1..=4096`), `descriptor_table_bytes(queue_size) -> Option<usize>` / `avail_ring_bytes(queue_size) -> Option<usize>` / `used_ring_bytes(queue_size) -> Option<usize>` con `checked_mul` + `checked_add` defence-in-depth. Test `rx_and_tx_queue_indices_match_spec`, `default_queue_depths_pass_validation`, `queue_depth_rejects_zero_and_above_max`, `queue_depth_rejects_non_power_of_two`, `descriptor_table_size_for_default_depth` (256 × 16 = 4096 anchor — esattamente una page), `avail_ring_size_for_default_depth` (6 + 256 × 2 = 518), `used_ring_size_for_default_depth` (6 + 256 × 8 = 2054), `queue_depth_accepts_full_range_boundaries` (1 e 4096 ambo power-of-2 in range). **Data snapshot precedente:** 2026-05-20 (**P6.7.8.0 CLOSED — `postcard` decoder per `DriverManifestV1` wired in `crates/omni-kernel/src/driver_manifest.rs`**). (1) **Wire-type split**: nuovo `DriverManifestBody { meta: DriverMetaBody, capabilities, matchers }` + `DriverMetaBody { name, version, omni_image_hash, omni_issuer_pubkey }` (postcard-serializable; deliberatamente esclude `omni_signature` perché una firma non può firmare sé stessa — OIP-013 § S5.3 step 5). `DriverManifest::body()` proietta la rappresentazione in-memory sul wire-body; `hydrate_manifest(body, signature) -> DriverManifest` ricostruisce dall'omni-pack envelope (signature section + manifest section sono due slice separate). (2) **`postcard_decode_manifest` wired** via `omni_types::wire::decode_canonical::<DriverManifestBody>(bytes)`: no-trailing-bytes invariant enforced per `OIP-Serde-004` (un attaccante non può smuggle dati extra past il signature pre-image — la decode rejection è la difesa); errore mapped a `DriverManifestError::MalformedPack` (POSIX `EINVAL` al syscall boundary). (3) **`verify_manifest` ora usa il canonical encoder**: `encode_canonical(&manifest.body())` sostituisce il vecchio `build_signing_payload` handcrafted (length-prefixed u32_le strings + TAG_MMIO/DMA/IRQ/PCI bytes + manual resource encoding). Il nuovo path è byte-deterministic, single-audit-point (tutto il workspace incanala postcard via `omni_types::wire`), e mandato dalla spec OIP-013 § S5.3 step 5. (4) **Cleanup**: rimossa `DriverManifestError::ParserNotWired` variant (non più necessaria — il parser ora c'è); rimossi 5 helper handcrafted (`build_signing_payload`, `push_lenprefixed_str`, `push_string_vec`, `push_resource_vec`, `encode_resource`, `push_pci_matchers`) e 4 TAG_* constants (`TAG_MMIO=0x10`, `TAG_DMA=0x11`, `TAG_IRQ=0x12`, `TAG_PCI=0x13`). Tutto sostituito dal canonical postcard di OIP-Serde-004. (5) **Serde derives**: `DriverCapabilities`, `DriverMatchers`, `PciMatcher`, `DriverManifestBody`, `DriverMetaBody` derivano ora `Serialize, Deserialize` (Resource/Action già le derivavano da P6.7.3); `DriverManifest`/`DriverMeta` deliberatamente NON le derivano — il field `omni_signature: [u8; 64]` non ha serde impl built-in (serde supporta `[u8; N]` solo fino a N=32 nativo), e il wire path corretto passa per `body()` + omni-pack signature section. (6) **Tests** +5 new host-side: `postcard_round_trip_manifest_body_preserves_fields` (encode → decode → hydrate identità), `postcard_decode_manifest_rejects_trailing_bytes` (no-trailing-bytes invariant), `postcard_decode_manifest_rejects_truncated_input`, `postcard_decode_manifest_rejects_empty_input`, `body_round_trip_through_omni_pack_envelope` (end-to-end: encode body → wrap in omni-pack → decode_omni_pack → postcard_decode_manifest → hydrate = original). Sostituiti 2 test handcrafted (`postcard_decode_manifest_returns_parser_not_wired` cancellato; `signing_payload_encodes_capability_subset` riscritto come `signing_payload_grows_with_capabilities` invariant length-based + nuovo `signing_payload_omits_signature_field` che documenta esplicitamente che due manifest con firme diverse hanno signing payload identico — protegge contro regressioni accidentali che includessero la firma nel signing payload). `build_signing_payload_is_deterministic` rinominato `signing_payload_is_deterministic`. Net: 19 driver_manifest tests → **21 driver_manifest tests pass**. (5) **`crates/omni-kernel/src/driver_manifest.rs`** (nuovo modulo). Schema types: `DriverManifest { meta, capabilities, matchers }`, `DriverMeta { name, version, omni_image_hash: [u8; HASH_LEN=32], omni_signature: [u8; SIGNATURE_LEN=64], omni_issuer: String }`, `DriverCapabilities`, `DriverMatchers`, `PciMatcher`, `DriverManifestError`. Entry-point `verify_manifest(manifest, image_bytes)` esegue: (a) `Blake3::hash(image_bytes) == manifest.meta.omni_image_hash` → `ImageHashMismatch`; (b) `lookup_issuer(&manifest.meta.omni_issuer)` → `UnknownIssuer`; (c) Ed25519 `verify` via `OmniVerifyingKey::from_bytes(&issuer.verifying_key)` su `build_signing_payload(manifest)` → `SignatureInvalid`. Helper `build_signing_payload` byte-deterministic encoding con tag stable per ogni Resource variant (TAG_MMIO=0x10, TAG_DMA=0x11, TAG_IRQ=0x12, TAG_PCI=0x13); l'encoder handcrafted è transitorio (postcard pass deferito a P6.7.8).
